---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Pikkukanava

###  Pikkukanava₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Pikkukanava* (little chnnel)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  10
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
